English

At the midday-pressing, when they have maintained contact similarly, he offers a spoonful on the ─Аhavan─лya with the verse, тАЬMay Vi┼Ыve Devas, Maruts and Indra not leave us at the midday pressing. Long-lived, speaking what is pleasing to them, may we enjoy the favour of the gods, sv─Бh─Б.”26 At the ─Аrbhava Pavam─Бna while they have maintained contact similarly, he offers a spoonful on the ─Аhavan─лya with the verse, тАЬThis third pressing belongs to the wise the sons of Sudhanvan who through holy order have set the goblets in motion. When they have attained heaven, let them bear our good offering to what is better, sv─Бh─Б.”27
It is indeed said, “Certain offerings are made in a marked place, others in an unmarked place. Those which are marked by the ─Аgh─Бra-libations are deemed as marked; those which pertain to Soma are unmarked. After having taken up the cup for Indra-V─Бyu, the Adhvaryu should pour down the ─Аgh─Бra libation.”28

He takes out three shoots out of the tied up Soma respectively with the formulas. “May Vasus pull thee out with the G─Бyatr─л metre; do thou go to dear place of Agni. May Rudras pull thee out with the Triс╣гс╣нubh metre; do thou go to the dear place of Indra. May Adityas pull thee out with the Jagat─л metre; do thou go to the dear place of the Vi┼Ыve Devas.”73 Having poured water into the Hotr╠е’s goblet from the Vasat─лvar─л waters, he stirs up that water with twelve formulas, “O bright one, I stir the bright for thee in the gladdening water; …… in the joyous ones; … in the Kotan─Бs; ….. in the new ones; … in the Reс╣г─лs; … in the Meс╣г─лs; …. in the roaring ones; …… in the all-supporting ones; … in the sweet ones; .. in the lofty ones;…. in the strong ones; … in the pure ones.” Having clasped the shoots into the Adabhya cup, he takes up (the Ad─Бbhya draught) with the verse, тАЬI take the bright for thee with the bright form of day with the rays of the sun. Herein the dread ones have moved themselves, the streams of the heaven consorted.”74 Having taken it up he stands with the formula, “The lofty form of the bull shines forth.”75 He comes up with the formula, “Soma goes in advance of Soma, the bright goes in advance of bright.”75 Having come up he makes an offering on the ─Аhavan─лya with the formula, тАЬO Soma, sv─Бh─Б to thee, Soma, whose name is unerring and watchful.”75 Having turned by the right, he inserts the shoots into the Soma respectively with the formulas, “O God Soma, striving, do thou go to the dear place of Agni with the G─Бyatri metre. O God Soma, willing do thou go to the dear place of Indra with the Triс╣гс╣нubh metre. O God Soma, our friend, do thou go to the dear place of the Vi┼Ыve Devas with the Jagat─л metre.76

He dashes hands against each other with the verse, тАЬOne is eater of what is offered, another is one who devours what is not offered; still another is one who consumes what is gathered. May they (the three fires) provide us with remedy, seat and delightful strength.”86 One purifies him (the bachelor) with three bunches of darbha-blades with eight verses :87

(i) The Soma which is being passed through the filter, which is born in the heaven and which is the beholder of every thing; may it, itself the purifier, purify me.

(ii) May the groups of gods purify me; may the men purify me through the intellect; may all living beings purify me.

(iii) O god J─Бtavedas Agni, do thou, shining, purify me like the filter, by thy brilliant filter following the good intentions.

(iv) O Agni, may we purify our divine song through thy filter which is spread amidst thy flame.

(v) O god Savitr╠е, may we purify this divine song through both the filter and the impulse.

(vi) May the goddess pertaining to all gods who purifies (everything) and who possesses several straight-backed bodies come (to us). Through her may we who rejoice in the convivial feasts, become masters of wealth.

(vii) May Vai┼Ыv─Бnara Agni purify me by his rays. may Vata who is refreshing and giving pleasure purify me through the vital breath. May Dy─Бv─Бpr╠еthiv─л who are lawful and holy purify me through water and other liquids.

(viii) Ogod Savitr╠е, (I pray thee) with extensive, spreading and highest prayers. O Agni, do thou purify me through thy powers.”

One who desires to know the year (suitable for a sacrificial session) gets up in the latter part of night which marks the beginning of yearly session (that is) the eighth day of the bright half of the month of Magha, bakes a cake of flour of paddy measuring four ┼Ъar─Бvas. Dried leaves are taken with it.

May the desires of the sacrificer come true.”97 While she is being made to lie down, he adds the formula, “Thou art the the goat firm in wealth; do thou be seated on the earth; do thou reach the midregion straight, let thy great lustre be in the heaven.”97

One who is going to offer Jaya- offerings procures a spoon and a ladle made of Badhaka wood, enclosing sticks of Badhaka wood, Barhis of Sara grass, faggot of Vibh─лdaka tree. Having kindled fire informally, having spread Barhis of ┼Ъara grass, having laid around the enclosing sticks of Badhaka wood, having besmeared the faggot of Vibh─лdaka tree and having put it (on the ─Аhavan─лya) with Sv─Бh─Б-utterance, he makes thirteen offerings, each time dipping the spoon into the vessel of clarified butter respectively with the formulas, cittaс╣Б ca sv─Бh─Б, citti┼Ы ca sv─Бh─Б etc. Alternatively, having taken up four spoonfuls into the ladle made of Badhaka wood with the spoon made of Badhaka wood, and having gone along all formulas together, he makes the offerings with the formulas, “(may I have) thought and thinking, intent and intention, known and knowledge, mind and power, the new-moon and the’ full-moon, Br╠еhat and Rathantara. Praj─Бpati bestowed victories on Indra the mighty, dread in battles; all people paid respect to him the dread; he has become worthy of offering, sv─Бh─Б.”99

English

He should offer Abhy─Бt─Бna offerings in that rite by which he may desire to prosper saying “let this rite of mine succed.” One who is going to offer the Abhy─Бt─Бna offerings procures a spoon and a ladle made of the wood of Butea frondosa, enclosing sticks of Butea frondosa, Barhis of Kusa grass and the faggot of Butea frondosa. Then having informally kindled fire, having spread the Barhis of Ku┼Ыa grass, having laid around the enclosing sticks of Butea frondosa, and having besmeared the faggot of Butea frondosa, he puts it on the ─Аhavan─лya with sv─Бh─Б- utterance, makes seventeen offerings each time dipping the spoon of Butea frondosa, (into the vessel of clarified butter) respectively with the formulas, “Agni is the lord of creatures: may he guard me in this spiritual power, in the ruling power, in this blessing, in the priesthood, in this rite, in this invocation to gods. Indra is the lord of elderly persons, may he… - Yama is the lord of the earth; may he …. - V─Бyu is the lord of the midregion; may he …. - S┼лrya is the lord of heaven; may he…… - Candramas is the lord of constellations: may he Br╠еhaspati is the lord of spiritual power; may he …… - Mitra is the lord of truths; may he …. - Varuс╣Зa is the lord of waters; may he…. - Ocean is the lord of streams; may he…-Food is the lord of lordships; may it… - Soma is the lord of plants; may he…- Savitr╠е is the lord of impulses; may he….-Rudra is the lord of cattle; may he…-Tvaс╣гс╣нr╠е is the lord of forms; - Maruts are the lords of may he …. - Viс╣гс╣Зu is the lord of mountains; may he groups; may they …”[^6-895] At the end he makes the sacrificer recite the formula, “O Fathers, grandfathers, further ones, nearer ones, living fathers, living grandfathers, do you help us…[^6-895] Then there is an offering with all these formulas recited together. One should first offer the Abhy─Бt─Бna offerings; then the Jaya and then the R─Бstrabhс╣Ыt. The next Anuv─Бka100 is the Br─Бhmaс╣Зa relating to these.

English

He similarly gives impulse upto the Aptory─Бma.

With the verse, “The evil demons destroying the sacrifice, who are seated on earth, may Agni protect me from them, may we go to those who did good deeds, Sv─Бh─Б.”123 Having taken up another four spoonfuls, he makes the offering again on the G─Бrhapatya with the verse, “The evil demons stealing the sacrifice.”123 He approaches the ─Аgn─лdhra chamber with the verse, “We have come O Mitra and Varuс╣Зa, noble ones, to the share of the nights which is yours, grasping the firmament, in the place of good deeds on the third ridge above the light of heaven.”123 Having entered the ─Аgn─лdhra chamber and having taken up four spoonfuls into the ladle, he makes an offering on the ─Аgn─лdhr─лya fire while the sacrificer has contacted him, with the verse, “The evil demons destroying the sacrifice who sit in the midregion; may V─Бyu guard me from them; may we go to them who did good deeds, sv─Бh─Б.”123 Having taken another four spoonfuls he makes an offering on the ─Аgn─лdhr─лya fire itself with the verse, “The evil demons stealing the sacrifice…”124 He goes towards the ─Аhavan─лya with the verse, “The nights of thine O Savitr╠е, which go, traversed by gods, between heaven and earth, with them and all your houses and offspring, do you first mounting the light, traverse the regions.”125

Having reached the ─Аhavan─лya and having taken four spoonfuls into the ladle, he makes an offering on the ─Аhavan─лya fire, while the sacrificer has maintained his contact, with the verse, “The evil demons destroying the sacrifice who are seated in the heaven, may S┼лrya protect me from them; may we go to them who have done good deeds, sv─Бh─Б.”125 Having taken another four spoonfuls he makes an offering on the ─Аhavan─лya itself with the verse, “The evil demons stealing the sacrifice who are seated in the heaven, may S┼лrya protect me from them; may we go to them who have done good deeds, sv─Бh─Б.”[^l-913]

Then he prays to the ─Аhavan─лya with the verse, тАЬO J─Бtavedas Agni, do thou feed this (sacrificer) with that best oblation with which thou didst provide Indra with milk (mixed with Soma). Do thou place him in superiority among his kinsmen.”125

  87. TBr. 1.4.8.1-3. The Anuv─Бka comprises seventeen verses out of which the first eight versrs have been employed herre. The Anuv─Бka is not employed for a specific purpose (a├▒arabhy─Бdh─лta). While the other ┼Ъrautas┼лtras belonging to the Taittiriya recension have employed this entire Anuv─Бka towards the purification of a Soma-sacrificer at his initiation, Baudh─Бyana has prescribed a part of it in a domestic rite (Sam─Гvartana) which is really speakig outside the scope of a ┼Ъrautas┼лtra. ↩︎
